I give this place a 1 star because of how dirty the restaurant was. The bathroom, the floors and the soda counter. Unfortunately, the restaurant was basically empty so I can't associate the blame to a busy croud. The is an A grade from the health department posted but if they came when we were there, that wouldn't be the case. I really like Baja Fresh and have never seen one this neglected. As I read through the reviews, this restaurant has had previous customers with the same cleanliness concerns.< /Text>

< review>
My husband raves about this place as when he's in the city working he comes here. Finally I was with him and he brought me. Fresh is right! Purple onion, red pepper, cotija, fresh avocado and grilled shrimp in this fantastic salad! Every bite chopped to the perfect size. I can't say enough about the dressing, SO much flavor. Remember to try the black salsa from the sparkling clean salsa bar. I'm not exaggerating! Never had black salsa and I don't  know how they make it but it's amazing with chips and on their wahoo tacos.</review>

< Review>
I came here for lunch while I was running an errand in Staples, since I haven't been to a Baja Fresh for the longest time. It's been ages since I had their food.  I decided to order their new Chicken Sandwich since from the photo, it looks tasty; so why not give it a try. I am so glad I ordered it.  The chicken pieces were large and the best part was that it wasn't dry or hard.   It had large chunks of Avocado, and a decent amount of lettuce.  I poured their hot salsa into the sandwich to give it an extra kick to the flavor. The sandwich tasted great. I was also enjoying their chips and salsa while waiting for my food.  Coming here really brought back memories of my childhood, when I used to come here just to eat their chips... hahaa..</Review>

<review>First off, service was excellent. The girl at the counter war super nice. Too bad the food was disappointing but that's not her fault. So one star for that.
I'm just about done with this place with their filling proportions. The chicken burrito that I usually order cost almost two dollars more here than the other location I used to go to. However the burrito size was exceptionally large by which I initially dismissed the high price. But when you get through the entire burrito just to experience 70% rice and maybe 20% veggies and 10% chicken you can't say the size of the burrito justifies the 9$ price tag. I had a very large filling burrito that tasted mostly of rice. Sorry but I'm not visiting another baja fresh again. < Review>
I must say, Truly Nolen strives to give excellent service, although they don't always quite get there. Several times service has been scheduled and either no one has showed or the time window was incorrect even though the main office put me on hold to confirm the day/time with the San Diego office and I was SURE about the time/day. They tell me they want to do an emergency service when a trap has a mouse or rat but when the technician comes out to get the dead animal, they either don't have peanut butter or don't have fresh traps to replace one if we had to throw it away due to waiting too long for someone to come. I do want to recognize on employee for his exceptional service, Manny, who willingly goes beyond the standard service if we ask. For example, it wasn't time for our seasonal service but I was noticing spiders in the house so he treated again. He knows where he set the traps, checks them all, always has peanut butter for them and extra traps if needed and even added wire to the edges of our garage door to keep the rats and mice from cruising in. When other technicians are scheduled for a follow-up service, I have to be home to show them where all the traps are or some are missed as my partner doesn't remember them all. A compliment to the office staff: they are always friendly, polite and trying hard to provide good service.
Update on 6-23-19: I also want to acknowledge German, who has been providing regular and excellent service more recently.</Review>

I must say, Truly Nolen strives to give excellent service, although they don't always quite get there. Several times service has been scheduled and either no one has showed or the time window was incorrect even though the main office put me on hold to confirm the day/time with the San Diego office and I was SURE about the time/day. They tell me they want to do an emergency service when a trap has a mouse or rat but when the technician comes out to get the dead animal, they either don't have peanut butter or don't have fresh traps to replace one if we had to throw it away due to waiting too long for someone to come. I do want to recognize on employee for his exceptional service, Manny, who willingly goes beyond the standard service if we ask. For example, it wasn't time for our seasonal service but I was noticing spiders in the house so he treated again. He knows where he set the traps, checks them all, always has peanut butter for them and extra traps if needed and even added wire to the edges of our garage door to keep the rats and mice from cruising in. When other technicians are scheduled for a follow-up service, I have to be home to show them where all the traps are or some are missed as my partner doesn't remember them all. A compliment to the office staff: they are always friendly, polite and trying hard to provide good service.
Update on 6-23-19: I also want to acknowledge German, who has been providing regular and excellent service more recently.</review>

< name>
Amos Glick< /name>
<Date>1493840260563<//Date>< Rating>
5</Rating>
< text>
I've been studying improvisation for thirty years and I can say without hesitation that Impro is a very special place. First and foremost their main company ensemble is one of the top in the U.S. and likely the world. Their space work, use of language, playfulness to the point of palpable danger, and writer's mindset is as invigorating and refreshing as any good piece of theatre should be. Secondly, as an experienced improviser I was very pleased that I was able to audition into an appropriate level for me and I have to say I was blown away by the skill and talent of the other students there. I love how Impro teaches the improviser to think like a writer; not that they should script the scene, but that every bit of dialogue, movement, and space work should be performed with the idea that the playwright wrote it because it's important... it has meaning. Unlike many other improv schools I've been to they employ techniques that groundbreaking theatre makers use such as Viewpoints and the Circles Of Presence; no wonder they are more and more being regarded as a theatre company and not just an improv troupe!</text>

<Review>We knew we needed a new Temper Pedic bed and we have had good experiences at this location when it was a SleepTrain on Blossom Hill. We knew it had merged with another company and were now "Mattress Firm", but we went in figuring we knew what brand of mattress we wanted (Temper Pedic), what type firmness and just wanted 2 adjustable sides of a King. What we discovered was that now there are many more options and types, especially of the bases. I figured we would be turning down anything that wasn't just simply for raising the head and feet. But then salesman Doug Kalpakoff began to really help us. He didn't just ask if we were side sleepers or back or stomach sleepers. He let us know how a choice in a base can affect circulation, sleep apnea issues, how age or weight affects how firm a mattress you want (he did so making fun of himself!). <review>Best tasting poke in Stockton. Very fresh, melt in your mouth fish. They sourced quality fish and sliced it properly so there is no gritty taste. We went during Restaurant week in Stockton. Small bowl of poke with one poke taco and a cream topped tea drink for $15. A good deal if you can still get it.

In terms of the portion size, I've had better elsewhere in the bay area and even tri-valley. The scooper they use was smallish and the scoop was not very large. The combo meal made me wanting more food as I wasn't full. They offer a large sized bowl but I didn't see a larger size bowl at the counter, instead it's 3 scoops for small and 4 scoops for large for a buck more. I'd pay more for a larger portion size.

Their fish is melt in your mouth good. The sauces they put on has the perfect amount of flavor. Their spicy items are not spicy at all but that's the way I prefer it. If you've ever had Boiling Crab, their spicy is like mild level at BC.

Their tea is the bomb. Any cream topped tea they offer, get it. Honestly their tea quality ranks up there with the best and it's good value. They have these awesome cups with a cap when you get cream topped foam with your tea. It seems like a lot of people just come for their tea.< /review><Pics>None<//Pics>< Response>

They even have live music nights and other events that they post to their social media outlets to keep people up to date and often run specials on new menu items to help spread the word and encourage people to try something other than their favorites.

<userid>116262773941620720888< /userid><pictures>None< /pictures>< text>
I'm originally from Detroit and spent a good amount of my Saturday nights in nearby Windsor, Ontario.  One of the best parts of that experience was being able to get some killer Lebanese food while watching Hockey Night In Canada.  Well, after driving down Brookhurst after running errands in the area, I noticed the sign for Sahara Falafel and was like "Hey, why not?"  I walked in on a Saturday night, saw they were playing Hockey Night In Canada on the TV, and immediately knew I was at the right place.  The service wasn't fast, but it was friendly and personable.  The food was awesome and left me feeling beyond full.  The beef shawarma plate was great and the option to substitute hummus for baba gannoush was very welcome from my perspective.  All and all, I found it to be quite enjoyable and will definitely be back in the future.<//text>

< Review>
I was not a happy camper at Sahara Falafel. I expected Middle Eastern food that would exceed my expectations, especially seeing as how its situated in Little Arabia. Sadly, that was not the case. I have had many Chicken Schwarmas in my life (at other places, even more Americanized Middle-Eastern joints,  and the one I had here at Sahara Falafel was the worst one I ever had. The pita bread was dry and the chicken was dry and had way too many spices on it!! The spices were so overpowering in my food and on my tastebuds; I had to rinse my mouth with Listerine three times to get rid of the taste of the terrible food. I feel extremely disappointed and strongly feel that I was incredibly mislead by all of the positive reviews I read on Yelp.</Review>
